db,\n109\t\t\tweatherAPIURL:   weatherURL,\n110\t\t\tquietHoursStart: 22, // 10pm\n111\t\t\tquietHoursEnd:   6,  // 6am\n112\t\t}, nil\n113\t}\n114\t\n115\t// SetQuietHours sets the quiet hours range for overnight events.\n116\tfunc (g *Generator) SetQuietHours(start, end int) {\n117\t\tg.quietHoursStart = start\n118\t\tg.quietHoursEnd = end\n119\t}\n120\t\n121\t// SetWeatherAPIURL sets the weather API URL for weather section.\n122\tfunc (g *Generator) SetWeatherAPIURL(url string) {\n123\t\tg.weatherAPIURL = url\n124\t}\n125\t\n126\t// Close closes the DB connection.\n127\tfunc (g *Generator) Close() error {\n128\t\treturn g.db.Close()\n129\t}\n130\t\n131\t// SetProviders sets the provider interfaces for briefing generation.\n132\tfunc (g *Generator) SetProviders(z ZoneProvider, p PersonProvider, pr PredictionProvider, h HealthProvider) {\n133\t\tg.zoneProvider = z\n134\t\tg.personProvider = p\n135\t\tg.predictionProvider = pr\n136\t\tg.healthProvider = h\n137\t}\n138\t\n139\t// SetNodeInfoProvider sets the node info provider.\n140\tfunc (g *Generator) SetNodeInfoProvider(n NodeInfoProvider) {\n141\t\tg.nodeProvider = n\n142\t}\n143\t\n144\t// DailyBriefing is the primary struct for a morning briefing.\n145\t// Alias for Briefing with additional delivery tracking fields.\n146\ttype DailyBriefing = Briefing\n147\t\n148\t// BriefingSectionType defines the type of briefing section.\n149\ttype BriefingSectionType string\n150\t\n151\tconst (\n152\t\tSectionTypeSleep           BriefingSectionType = \"sleep\"\n153\t\tSectionTypeOvernightEvents BriefingSectionType = \"overnight_events\"\n154\t\tSectionTypeSystemHealth    BriefingSectionType = \"system_health\"\n155\t\tSectionTypePredictions     BriefingSectionType = \"predictions\"\n156\t\tSectionTypeWeather         BriefingSectionType = \"weather\"\n157\t\tSectionTypeAlert           BriefingSectionType = \"alert\"\n158\t\tSectionTypePeople          BriefingSectionType = \"people\"\n159\t\tSectionTypeAnomaly         BriefingSectionType = \"anomaly\"\n160\t\tSectionTypeLearning        BriefingSectionType = \"learning\"\n161\t)\n162\t\n163\t// Briefing holds a generated morning briefing.\n164\ttype Briefing struct {\n165\t\tID           string            `json:\"id\"` // UUID\n166\t\tDate         string            `json:\"date\"`\n167\t\tPerson       string            `json:\"person,omitempty\"`\n168\t\tContent      string            `json:\"content\"`\n169\t\tGeneratedAt  int64             `json:\"generated_at\"`\n170\t\tSections     []Section         `json:\"sections,omitempty\"`\n171\t\tDelivered    bool              `json:\"delivered\"`          // Set true after first push\n172\t\tAcknowledged bool              `json:\"acknowledged\"`       // Set true when user dismisses\n173\t\tMetadata     map[string]string `json:\"metadata,omitempty\"` // Additional metadata\n174\t}\n175\t\n176\t// Section represents a single section of the briefing.\n177\ttype Section struct {\n178\t\tType     BriefingSectionType `json:\"type\"`\n179\t\tContent  string              `json:\"content\"`\n180\t\tPriority int                 `json:\"priority\"`           // Higher = shown first\n181\t\tSeverity string              `json:\"severity,omitempty\"` // For alerts: \"info\", \"warning\", \"error\"\n182\t}\n183\t\n184\t// Generate creates a morning briefing for the given date and person.\n185\t// If person is empty, generates a household-wide briefing.\n186\tfunc (g *Generator) Generate(date string, person string) (*Briefing, error) {\n187\t\tvar sections []Section\n188\t\n189\t\t// Parse date for calculations\n190\t\tdateTime, err := time.Parse(\"2006-01-02\", date)\n191\t\tif err != nil {\n192\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"parse date: %w\", err)\n193\t\t}\n194\t\n195\t\t// Calculate time range for \"last night\" (previous day 18:00 to current day 06:00)\n196\t\t// This covers the overnight period including early morning hours\n197\t\tnightStart := time.Date(dateTime.Year(), dateTime.Month(), dateTime.Day()-1, 18, 0, 0, 0, time.Local)\n198\t\tnightEnd := time.Date(dateTime.Year(), dateTime.Month(), dateTime.Day(), 6, 0, 0, 0, time.Local)\n199\t\n200\t\t// BLOCK 1 — Critical alerts (fall, security)\n201\t\tif alertSection := g.generateAlertBlock(nightStart, nightEnd, person); alertSection != nil {\n202\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *alertSection)\n203\t\t}\n204\t\n205\t\t// BLOCK 2 — Sleep summary\n206\t\tif sleepSection := g.generateSleepBlock(date, person); sleepSection != nil {\n207\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *sleepSection)\n208\t\t}\n209\t\n210\t\t// BLOCK 3 — Who is home (current state)\n211\t\tif peopleSection := g.generatePeopleBlock(person); peopleSection != nil {\n212\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *peopleSection)\n213\t\t}\n214\t\n215\t\t// BLOCK 4 — Overnight events (replaces anomaly block with more detailed filtering)\n216\t\tif overnightSection := g.generateOvernightEventsBlock(nightStart, nightEnd, person); overnightSection != nil {\n217\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *overnightSection)\n218\t\t}\n219\t\n220\t\t// BLOCK 5 — System health\n221\t\tif healthSection := g.generateHealthBlock(); healthSection != nil {\n222\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *healthSection)\n223\t\t}\n224\t\n225\t\t// BLOCK 6 — Weather (optional)\n226\t\tif weatherSection := g.generateWeatherBlock(); weatherSection != nil {\n227\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *weatherSection)\n228\t\t}\n229\t\n230\t\t// BLOCK 7 — Prediction hint\n231\t\tif predictionSection := g.generatePredictionBlock(person); predictionSection != nil {\n232\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *predictionSection)\n233\t\t}\n234\t\n235\t\t// BLOCK 8 — Learning progress\n236\t\tif learningSection := g.generateLearningBlock(); learningSection != nil {\n237\t\t\tsections = append(sections, *learningSection)\n238\t\t}\n239\t\n240\t\t// Degenerate case\n241\t\tif len(sections) == 0 {\n242\t\t\tsections = append(sections, Section{\n243\t\t\t\tType:     \"info\",\n244\t\t\t\tContent:  \"All quiet last night. All systems healthy.\",\n245\t\t\t\tPriority: 0,\n246\t\t\t})\n247\t\t}\n248\t\n249\t\t// Sort by priority descending\n250\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(sections)-1; i++ {\n251\t\t\tfor j := i + 1; j < len(sections); j++ {\n252\t\t\t\tif sections[j].Priority > sections[i].Priority {\n253\t\t\t\t\tsections[i], sections[j] = sections[j], sections[i]\n254\t\t\t\t}\n255\t\t\t}\n256\t\t}\n257\t\n258\t\t// Build content from prioritized sections\n259\t\tcontentParts := make([]string, 0, len(sections))\n260\t\tfor _, s := range sections {\n261\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, s.Content)\n262\t\t}\n263\t\tcontent := strings.Join(contentParts, \"\\n\\n\")\n264\t\n265\t\treturn &Briefing{\n266\t\t\tID:           uuid.New().String(),\n267\t\t\tDate:         date,\n268\t\t\tPerson:       person,\n269\t\t\tContent:      content,\n270\t\t\tGeneratedAt:  time.Now().UnixMilli(),\n271\t\t\tSections:     sections,\n272\t\t\tDelivered:    false,\n273\t\t\tAcknowledged: false,\n274\t\t}, nil\n275\t}\n276\t\n277\t// generateAlertBlock generates BLOCK 1 — Critical alerts.\n278\tfunc (g *Generator) generateAlertBlock(nightStart, nightEnd time.Time, person string) *Section {\n279\t\tquery := `SELECT type, zone, person, detail_json, severity\n280\t\t           FROM events\n281\t\t           WHERE timestamp_ms >= ? AND timestamp_ms < ?\n282\t\t             AND type IN ('fall_alert', 'security_alert')\n283\t\t             AND severity IN ('alert', 'critical')`\n284\t\targs := []interface{}{nightStart.UnixMilli(), nightEnd.UnixMilli()}\n285\t\n286\t\tif person != \"\" {\n287\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n288\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n289\t\t}\n290\t\tquery += ` ORDER BY timestamp_ms ASC LIMIT 5`\n291\t\n292\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Alert query: nightStart=%s (%d), nightEnd=%s (%d), person=%s\",\n293\t\t\tnightStart, nightStart.UnixMilli(), nightEnd, nightEnd.UnixMilli(), person)\n294\t\n295\t\trows, err := g.db.Query(query, args...)\n296\t\tif err != nil {\n297\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Alert query error: %v\", err)\n298\t\t\treturn nil\n299\t\t}\n300\t\tdefer rows.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n301\t\n302\t\tvar alerts []string\n303\t\tfor rows.Next() {\n304\t\t\tvar eventType, zone, personName, detailJSON, severity string\n305\t\t\tif err := rows.Scan(&eventType, &zone, &personName, &detailJSON, &severity); err != nil {\n306\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Scan error: %v\", err)\n307\t\t\t\tcontinue\n308\t\t\t}\n309\t\n310\t\t\tvar alert strings.Builder\n311\t\t\tswitch eventType {\n312\t\t\tcase \"fall_alert\":\n313\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(\"⚠ Fall detected\")\n314\t\t\t\tif personName != \"\" {\n315\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(\": \")\n316\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(personName)\n317\t\t\t\t}\n318\t\t\t\tif zone != \"\" {\n319\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(\" in \")\n320\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(zone)\n321\t\t\t\t}\n322\t\t\tcase \"security_alert\":\n323\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(\"⚠ Security alert\")\n324\t\t\t\tif zone != \"\" {\n325\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(\": Motion in \")\n326\t\t\t\t\talert.WriteString(zone)\n327\t\t\t\t}\n328\t\t\t}\n329\t\t\talerts = append(alerts, alert.String())\n330\t\t}\n331\t\n332\t\tif len(alerts) == 0 {\n333\t\t\treturn nil\n334\t\t}\n335\t\n336\t\tcontent := \"⚠ \" + strings.Join(alerts, \"; \")\n337\t\tif len(alerts) > 1 {\n338\t\t\tcontent = fmt.Sprintf(\"⚠ %d critical events overnight. \", len(alerts)) + strings.Join(alerts, \"; \")\n339\t\t}\n340\t\n341\t\treturn &Section{\n342\t\t\tType:     \"alert\",\n343\t\t\tContent:  content,\n344\t\t\tPriority: 100,\n345\t\t}\n346\t}\n347\t\n348\t// generateSleepBlock generates BLOCK 2 — Sleep summary.\n349\tfunc (g *Generator) generateSleepBlock(date, person string) *Section {\n350\t\tquery := `SELECT duration_min, onset_latency_min, restlessness,\n351\t\t                 breathing_rate_avg, breathing_regularity, breathing_anomaly,\n352\t\t                 breathing_samples_json, person\n353\t\t           FROM sleep_records WHERE date = ?`\n354\t\targs := []interface{}{date}\n355\t\tif person != \"\" {\n356\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n357\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n358\t\t}\n359\t\n360\t\trows, err := g.db.Query(query, args...)\n361\t\tif err != nil {\n362\t\t\treturn nil\n363\t\t}\n364\t\tdefer rows.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n365\t\n366\t\tvar sleepRecords []struct {\n367\t\t\tDuration      sql.NullInt32\n368\t\t\tOnsetLatency  sql.NullFloat64\n369\t\t\tRestlessness  sql.NullFloat64\n370\t\t\tBreathAvg     sql.NullFloat64\n371\t\t\tBreathReg     sql.NullFloat64\n372\t\t\tBreathAnomaly sql.NullBool\n373\t\t\tBreathSamples sql.NullString\n374\t\t\tPerson        sql.NullString\n375\t\t}\n376\t\n377\t\tfor rows.Next() {\n378\t\t\tvar r struct {\n379\t\t\t\tDuration &r.OnsetLatency, &r.Restlessness,\n389\t\t\t\t&r.BreathAvg, &r.BreathReg, &r.BreathAnomaly, &r.BreathSamples, &r.Person); err != nil {\n390\t\t\t\tcontinue\n391\t\t\t}\n392\t\t\tsleepRecords = use the first record\n401\t\tr := sleepRecords[0]\n402\t\n403\t\tvar parts []string\n404\t\tpersonName := \"You\"\n405\t\tif r.Person.Valid && r.Person.String != \"\" {\n406\t\t\tpersonName = r.Person.String\n407\t\t}\n408\t\n409\t\t// Duration and deviation from average\n410\t\tif r.Duration.Valid && r.Duration.Int32 > 0 {\n411\t\t\th := r.Duration.Int32 / 60\n412\t\t\tm := r.Duration.Int32 % 60\n413\t\t\tif m > 0 {\n414\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s slept %dh %dm\", personName, h, m))\n415\t\t\t} else {\n416\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s slept %dh\", personName, h))\n417\t\t\t}\n418\t\n419\t\t\t// Compare with average (get from recent records)\n420\t\t\tavgDuration := g.getAverageSleepDuration(r.Person.String)\n421\t\t\tif avgDuration > 0 {\n422\t\t\t\tdelta := int(r.Duration.Int32) - avgDuration\n423\t\t\t\tif math.Abs(float64(delta)) >= 10 {\n424\t\t\t\t\tif delta > 0 {\n425\t\t\t\t\t\tparts[len(parts)-1] += fmt.Sprintf(\" — %d minutes more than your average\", delta)\n426\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n427\t\t\t\t\t\tparts[len(parts)-1] += fmt.Sprintf(\" — %d minutes less than your average\", -delta)\n428\t\t\t\t\t}\n429\t\t\t\t}\n430\t\t\t}\n431\t\t} else {\n432\t\t\tparts = append(parts, personName+\" slept\")\n433\t\t}\n434\t\n435\t\t// Restlessness\n436\t\tif r.Restlessness.Valid {\n437\t\t\tswitch {\n438\t\t\tcase r.Restlessness.Float64 < 1:\n439\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Restlessness: Low.\")\n440\t\t\tcase r.Restlessness.Float64 < 3:\n441\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Restlessness: Moderate.\")\n442\t\t\tdefault:\n443\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Restlessness: High.\")\n444\t\t\t}\n445\t\t}\n446\t\n447\t\t// Breathing regularity\n448\t\tif r.BreathReg.Valid {\n449\t\t\tcv := r.BreathReg.Float64\n450\t\t\tswitch {\n451\t\t\tcase cv < 0.10:\n452\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Breathing: Regular.\")\n453\t\t\tcase cv > 0.25:\n454\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Breathing: Irregular.\")\n455\t\t\tdefault:\n456\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, \"Breathing: Normal.\")\n457\t\t\t}\n458\t\t}\n459\t\n460\t\t// Breathing anomaly\n461\t\tif r.BreathAnomaly.Valid && r.BreathAnomaly.Bool {\n462\t\t\tif r.BreathSamples.Valid {\n463\t\t\t\tvar info map[string]interface{}\n464\t\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(r.BreathSamples.String), &info); err == nil {\n465\t\t\t\t\tavg, _ := info[\"avg\"].(float64)\n466\t\t\t\t\tpersonal, _ := info[\"personal_avg\"].(float64)\n467\t\t\t\t\tif personal > 0 {\n468\t\t\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Breathing rate elevated (%.0f bpm vs. %.0f bpm average).\",\n469\t\t\t\t\t\t\tavg, personal))\n470\t\t\t\t\t} else if avg > 0 {\n471\t\t\t\t\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Breathing rate elevated (%.0f bpm).\", avg))\n472\t\t\t\t\t}\n473\t\t\t\t}\n474\t\t\t}\n475\t\t}\n476\t\n477\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n478\t\t\treturn nil\n479\t\t}\n480\t\n481\t\treturn &Section{\n482\t\t\tType:     \"sleep\",\n483\t\t\tContent:  strings.Join(parts, \" \"),\n484\t\t\tPriority: 80,\n485\t\t}\n486\t}\n487\t\n488\t// generatePeopleBlock generates BLOCK 3 — Who is home.\n489\tfunc (g *Generator) generatePeopleBlock(person string) *Section {\n490\t\tif g.personProvider == nil {\n491\t\t\treturn nil\n492\t\t}\n493\t\n494\t\tpeopleHome := g.personProvider.GetPeopleHome()\n495\t\tif len(peopleHome) == 0 {\n496\t\t\treturn &Section{\n497\t\t\t\tType:     \"people\",\n498\t\t\t\tContent:  \"The house is currently empty.\",\n499\t\t\t\tPriority: 60,\n500\t\t\t}\n501\t\t}\n502\t\n503\t\tvar content string\n504\t\tif len(peopleHome) == 1 {\n505\t\t\tcontent = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s is home.\", peopleHome[0])\n506\t\t} Overnight anomalies.\n520\tfunc (g *Generator) generateAnomalyBlock(nightStart, nightEnd time.Time, person string) *Section {\n521\t\tquery := `SELECT type, zone, detail_json, timestamp_ms\n522\t\t           FROM events\n523\t\t           WHERE timestamp_ms >= ? AND timestamp_ms < ?\n524\t\t             AND type IN ('anomaly', 'unusual_activity')\n525\t\t             AND severity IN ('warning', 'alert')\n526\t\t           ORDER BY timestamp_ms ASC`\n527\t\targs := []interface{}{nightStart.UnixMilli(), nightEnd.UnixMilli()}\n528\t\n529\t\tif person != \"\" {\n530\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n531\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n532\t\t}\n533\t\tquery += ` LIMIT 3`\n534\t\n535\t\trows, err := g.db.Query(query, args...)\n536\t\tif err != nil {\n537\t\t\treturn nil\n538\t\t}\n539\t\tdefer rows.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n540\t\n541\t\tvar anomalies []string\n542\t\tfor rows.Next() {\n543\t\t\tvar eventType, zone, detailJSON string\n544\t\t\tvar timestamp int64\n545\t\t\tif err := rows.Scan(&eventType, &zone, &detailJSON, &timestamp); err != nil {\n546\t\t\t\tcontinue\n547\t\t\t}\n548\t\n549\t\t\t// Parse anomaly score from detail_json\n550\t\t\tvar detail map[string]interface{}\n551\t\t\tvar score float64\n552\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(detailJSON), &detail); err == nil {\n553\t\t\t\tif s, ok := detail[\"score\"].(float64); ok {\n554\t\t\t\t\tscore = s\n555\t\t\t\t}\n556\t\t\t}\n557\t\n558\t\t\ttimeStr := time.Unix(0, timestamp*1e6).Format(\"3:04pm\")\n559\t\t\tvar anomaly strings.Builder\n560\t\t\tif zone != \"\" {\n561\t\t\t\tanomaly.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Motion in %s at %s\", zone, timeStr))\n562\t\t\t} else {\n563\t\t\t\tanomaly.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Unusual activity at %s\", timeStr))\n564\t\t\t}\n565\t\n566\t\t\tif score >= 0.85 {\n567\t\t\t\tanomaly.WriteString(\". High-confidence.\")\n568\t\t\t} else if score < 0.7 {\n569\t\t\t\tanomaly.WriteString(\". Likely environmental.\")\n570\t\t\t}\n571\t\n572\t\t\tanomalies = append(anomalies, anomaly.String())\n573\t\t}\n574\t\n575\t\tif len(anomalies) == 0 {\n576\t\t\treturn nil\n577\t\t}\n578\t\n579\t\tvar content string\n580\t\tif len(anomalies) == 1 {\n581\t\t\tcontent = \"Last night: \" + anomalies[0]\n582\t\t} else {\n583\t\t\tcontent = fmt.Sprintf(\"Last night: %d unusual events. Most notable: \", len(anomalies)) + anomalies[0]\n584\t\t}\n585\t\n586\t\treturn &Section{\n587\t\t\tType:     \"anomaly\",\n588\t\t\tContent:  content,\n589\t\t\tPriority: 70,\n590\t\t}\n591\t}\n592\t\n593\t// generateHealthBlock generates BLOCK 5 — System health.\n594\tfunc (g *Generator) generateHealthBlock() *Section {\n595\t\tif g.healthProvider == nil int(duration.Hours())\n622\t\t\t\t\t\tdurationM := int(duration.Minutes()) % 60\n623\t\t\t\t\t\tif durationH > 0 {\n624\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif durationM > 0 {\n625\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Node %s has been offline for %dh %dm.\", name, durationH, durationM))\n626\t\t\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n627\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Node %s has been offline for %dh.\", name, durationH))\n628\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n629\t\t\t\t\t\t} else if durationM > 0 {\n630\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Node %s has been offline for %dmin.\", name, durationM))\n631\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n632\t\t\t\t\t}\n633\t\t\t\t}\n634\t\t\t}\n635\t\t}\n636\t\n637\t\t// Add detection quality if not excellent\n638\t\tif quality < 90 {\n639\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Detection quality: %.0f%%.\", quality))\n640\t\t}\n641\t\n642\t\t// Skip if everything is healthy\n643\t\tif len(contentParts) == 1 && online == total && quality >= 90 {\n644\t\t\treturn nil\n645\t\t}\n646\t\n647\t\tcontent := strings.Join(contentParts, \" \")\n648\t\n649\t\treturn &Section{\n650\t\t\tType:     SectionTypeSystemHealth,\n651\t\t\tContent:  content,\n652\t\t\tPriority: 30,\n653\t\t}\n654\t}\n655\t\n656\t// generatePredictionBlock generates BLOCK 6 — Prediction hint.\n657\tfunc (g *Generator) generatePredictionBlock(person string) *Section {\n658\t\tif g.predictionProvider == nil {\n659\t\t\treturn nil\n660\t\t}\n661\t\n662\t\t// Get prediction for next action (15 min horizon)\n663\t\tzone, probability, ok := g.predictionProvider.GetPrediction(person, 15)\n664\t\tif !ok || probability < 0.7 {\n665\t\t\treturn nil\n666\t\t}\n667\t\n668\t\t// Format day of week\n669\t\tnow := time.Now()\n670\t\tdayOfWeek := now.Weekday().String()\n671\t\n672\t\t// Find what action this prediction suggests\n673\t\tcontent := fmt.Sprintf(\"Today's forecast: Based on your %s pattern, you'll likely be in %s in 15 minutes (%.0f%% confidence).\",\n674\t\t\tdayOfWeek, zone, probability*100)\n675\t\n676\t\treturn &Section{\n677\t\t\tType:     \"prediction\",\n678\t\t\tContent:  content,\n679\t\t\tPriority: 40,\n680\t\t}\n681\t}\n682\t\n683\t// generateLearningBlock generates BLOCK 7 — Learning progress.\n684\tfunc (g *Generator) generateLearningBlock() *Section {\n685\t\tif g.healthProvider == nil {\n686\t\t\treturn nil\n687\t\t}\n688\t\n689\t\tdelta, feedbackCount := g.healthProvider.GetAccuracyDelta()\n690\t\tif feedbackCount == 0 {\n691\t\t\treturn nil\n692\t\t}\n693\t\n694\t\tvar content string\n695\t\tif delta > 0 {\n696\t\t\tcontent = fmt.Sprintf(\"Accuracy improved %.0f%% this week thanks to your %d corrections.\",\n697\t\t\t\tdelta, feedbackCount)\n698\t\t} else {\n699\t\t\tcontent = fmt.Sprintf(\"You provided %d corrections this week.\", feedbackCount)\n700\t\t}\n701\t\n702\t\treturn &Section{\n703\t\t\tType:     SectionTypeLearning,\n704\t\t\tContent:  content,\n705\t\t\tPriority: 20,\n706\t\t}\n707\t}\n708\t\n709\t// generateOvernightEventsBlock generates the overnight events section.\n710\t// Filters for FallDetected, AnomalyDetected, NodeDisconnected events during quiet hours.\n711\tfunc (g *Generator) generateOvernightEventsBlock(nightStart, nightEnd time.Time, person string) *Section {\n712\t\t// Calculate quiet hours period\n713\t\t// Use the passed time range directly (already calculated as 18:00 previous day to 06:00 current day)\n714\t\n715\t\tquery := `SELECT type, zone, person, detail_json, timestamp_ms, severity\n716\t\t           FROM events\n717\t\t           WHERE timestamp_ms >= ? AND timestamp_ms < ?\n718\t\t\t             AND type IN ('fall_alert', 'anomaly', 'node_disconnected')\n719\t\t\t             AND severity IN ('warning', 'alert', 'critical')\n720\t\t           ORDER BY timestamp_ms ASC\n721\t\t           LIMIT 6`\n722\t\n723\t\targs := []interface{}{nightStart.UnixMilli(), nightEnd.UnixMilli()}\n724\t\n725\t\tif person != \"\" {\n726\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n727\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n728\t\t}\n729\t\n730\t\trows, err := g.db.Query(query, args...)\n731\t\tif err != nil {\n732\t\t\treturn nil\n733\t\t}\n734\t\tdefer rows.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n735\t\n736\t\tvar events []struct {\n737\t\t\tType       string\n738\t\t\tZone       string\n739\t\t\tPerson     string\n740\t\t\tDetailJSON string\n741\t\t\tTimestamp  int64\n742\t\t\tSeverity   string\n743\t\t\tAcked      bool\n744\t\t}\n745\t\n746\t\tfor rows.Next() {\n747\t\t\tvar e struct {\n748\t\t\t\tType       string\n749\t\t\t\tZone       string\n750\t\t\t\tPerson     string\n751\t\t\t\tDetailJSON string\n752\t\t\t\tTimestamp  int64\n753\t\t\t\tSeverity   string\n754\t\t\t\tAcked      bool\n755\t\t\t}\n756\t\t\tif err := rows.Scan(&e.Type, &e.Zone, &e.Person, &e.DetailJSON, &e.Timestamp, &e.Severity); err != nil {\n757\t\t\t\tcontinue\n758\t\t\t}\n759\t\n760\t\t\t// Check if acknowledged from detail_json\n761\t\t\tvar detail map[string]interface{}\n762\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(e.DetailJSON), &detail); err == nil {\n763\t\t\t\tif acked, ok := detail[\"acknowledged\"].(bool); ok {\n764\t\t\t\t\te.Acked = acked\n765\t\t\t\t}\n766\t\t\t}\n767\t\n768\t\t\tevents = append(events, e)\n769\t\t}\n770\t\n771\t\tif len(events) == 0 {\n772\t\t\treturn &Section{\n773\t\t\t\tType:     SectionTypeOvernightEvents,\n774\t\t\t\tContent:  \"No incidents overnight.\",\n775\t\t\t\tPriority: 40,\n776\t\t\t}\n777\t\t}\n778\t\n779\t\tvar contentParts []string\n780\t\tfor i, e := range events {\n781\t\t\tvar eventStr strings.Builder\n782\t\t\ttimeStr := time.Unix(0, e.Timestamp*1e6).Format(\"3:04pm\")\n783\t\n784\t\t\tswitch e.Type {\n785\t\t\tcase \"fall_alert\":\n786\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Possible fall detected at %s\", timeStr))\n787\t\t\t\tif e.Person != \"\" {\n788\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\" for %s\", e.Person))\n789\t\t\t\t}\n790\t\t\t\tif e.Zone != \"\" {\n791\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\" in %s\", e.Zone))\n792\t\t\t\t}\n793\t\t\t\tif e.Acked {\n794\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(\" (acknowledged)\")\n795\t\t\t\t}\n796\t\n797\t\t\tcase \"anomaly\":\n798\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Anomaly detected at %s\", timeStr))\n799\t\t\t\tif e.Zone != \"\" {\n800\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\" in %s\", e.Zone))\n801\t\t\t\t}\n802\t\t\t\tif e.Acked {\n803\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(\" (acknowledged)\")\n804\t\t\t\t}\n805\t\n806\t\t\tcase \"node_disconnected\":\n807\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Node %s went offline at %s\", e.Zone, timeStr))\n808\t\t\t\t// Try to get reconnection time\n809\t\t\t\tvar reconnectTime sql.NullInt64\n810\t\t\t\treconnectQuery := `SELECT timestamp_ms FROM events\n811\t\t\t\t                   WHERE type = 'node_connected' AND zone = ?\n812\t\t\t\t                   AND timestamp_ms > ? ORDER BY timestamp_ms ASC LIMIT 1`\n813\t\t\t\terr := g.db.QueryRow(reconnectQuery, e.Zone, e.Timestamp).Scan(&reconnectTime)\n814\t\t\t\tif err == nil && reconnectTime.Valid {\n815\t\t\t\t\treconnectStr := time.Unix(0, reconnectTime.Int64*1e6).Format(\"3:04pm\")\n816\t\t\t\t\teventStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\" and reconnected at %s\", reconnectStr))\n817\t\t\t\t}\n818\t\t\t}\n819\t\n820\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, eventStr.String())\n821\t\n822\t\t\t// Limit to 5 events\n823\t\t\tif i >= 4 && len(events) > 5 {\n824\t\t\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"...and %d more events.\", len(events)-5))\n825\t\t\t\tbreak\n826\t\t\t}\n827\t\t}\n828\t\n829\t\tcontent := strings.Join(contentParts, \". \")\n830\t\tif len(contentParts) > 1 {\n831\t\t\tcontent += \".\"\n832\t\t}\n833\t\n834\t\treturn &Section{\n835\t\t\tType:     SectionTypeOvernightEvents,\n836\t\t\tContent:  content,\n837\t\t\tPriority: 75,\n838\t\t}\n839\t}\n840\t\n841\t// generateWeatherBlock generates the optional weather section.\n842\tfunc (g *Generator) generateWeatherBlock() *Section {\n843\t\tif g.weatherAPIURL == \"\" {\n844\t\t\treturn nil\n845\t\t}\n846\t\n847\t\t// Fetch weather from wttr.in\n848\t\t// Format: GET https://wttr.in/{location}?format=%t+%C\n849\t\tclient := &http.Client{Timeout: 10 * time.Second}\n850\t\tresp, err := client.Get(g.weatherAPIURL)\n851\t\tif err != nil {\n852\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Failed to fetch weather: %v\", err)\n853\t\t\treturn nil\n854\t\t}\n855\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n856\t\n857\t\tif resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {\n858\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Weather API returned status %d\", resp.StatusCode)\n859\t\t\treturn nil\n860\t\t}\n861\t\n862\t\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n863\t\tif err != nil {\n864\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Failed to read weather response: %v\", err)\n865\t\t\treturn nil\n866\t\t}\n867\t\n868\t\tweather := strings.TrimSpace(string(body))\n869\t\tif weather == \"\" || weather == \"Unknown\" {\n870\t\t\treturn nil\n871\t\t}\n872\t\n873\t\treturn &Section{\n874\t\t\tType:     SectionTypeWeather,\n875\t\t\tContent:  fmt.Sprintf(\"Outside: %s\", weather),\n876\t\t\tPriority: 15,\n877\t\t}\n878\t}\n879\t\n880\t// getAverageSleepDuration calculates average sleep duration over the past 7 days.\n881\tfunc (g *Generator) getAverageSleepDuration(person string) int {\n882\t\tquery := `SELECT AVG(duration_min) FROM sleep_records\n883\t\t           WHERE date >= date('now', '-7 days')`\n884\t\targs := []interface{}{}\n885\t\tif person != \"\" {\n886\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n887\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n888\t\t}\n889\t\n890\t\tvar avg sql.NullFloat64\n891\t\terr := g.db.QueryRow(query, args...).Scan(&avg)\n892\t\tif err != nil || !avg.Valid {\n893\t\t\treturn 0\n894\t\t}\n895\t\treturn int(avg.Float64)\n896\t}\n897\t\n898\t// Save persists a briefing to the briefings table.\n899\tfunc (g *Generator) Save(b *Briefing) error {\n900\t\t// Check which columns exist in the briefings table\n901\t\tvar personColExists, sectionsJSONColExists bool\n902\t\n903\t\t// Check for person column\n904\t\terr := g.db.QueryRow(`\n905\t\t\tSELECT COUNT(*) > 0 FROM pragma_table_info('briefings') WHERE name = 'person'\n906\t\t`).Scan(&personColExists)\n907\t\tif err != nil {\n908\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"check person column: %w\", err)\n909\t\t}\n910\t\n911\t\t// Check for sections_json column\n912\t\terr = g.db.QueryRow(`\n913\t\t\tSELECT COUNT(*) > 0 FROM pragma_table_info('briefings') WHERE name = 'sections_json'\n914\t\t`).Scan(&sectionsJSONColExists)\n915\t\tif err != nil {\n916\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"check sections_json column: %w\", err)\n917\t\t}\n918\t\n919\t\t// Build query dynamically based on available columns\n920\t\tif personColExists && sectionsJSONColExists {\n921\t\t\t// Marshal sections to JSON if present\n922\t\t\tvar sectionsJSON sql.NullString\n923\t\t\tif len(b.Sections) > 0 {\n924\t\t\t\tdata, err := json.Marshal(b.Sections)\n925\t\t\t\tif err == nil {\n926\t\t\t\t\tsectionsJSON = sql.NullString{String: string(data), Valid: true}\n927\t\t\t\t}\n928\t\t\t}\n929\t\n930\t\t\t_, err = g.db.Exec(`\n931\t\t\t\tINSERT OR REPLACE INTO briefings (date, person, content, generated_at, sections_json)\n932\t\t\t\tVALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n933\t\t\t`, b.Date, b.Person, b.Content, b.GeneratedAt, sectionsJSON)\n934\t\t\treturn err\n935\t\t}\n936\t\n937\t\t// Fallback for old schema without person and sections_json\n938\t\t_, err = g.db.Exec(`\n939\t\t\tINSERT OR REPLACE INTO briefings (date, content, generated_at)\n940\t\t\tVALUES (?, ?, ?)\n941\t\t`, b.Date, b.Content, b.GeneratedAt)\n942\t\treturn err\n943\t}\n944\t\n945\t// Get retrieves a previously generated briefing by date and optional person.\n946\tfunc (g *Generator) Get(date string, person string) (*Briefing, error) {\n947\t\t// First, try to query with sections_json (new schema)\n948\t\tvar content string\n949\t\tvar generatedAt int64\n950\t\tvar personVal sql.NullString\n951\t\tvar sectionsJSON sql.NullString\n952\t\n953\t\tquery := `SELECT content, generated_at, person, sections_json FROM briefings WHERE date = ?`\n954\t\targs := []interface{}{date}\n955\t\n956\t\tif person != \"\" {\n957\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n958\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n959\t\t} else {\n960\t\t\tquery += ` AND (person IS NULL OR person = '')`\n961\t\t}\n962\t\n963\t\terr := g.db.QueryRow(query, args...).Scan(&content, &generatedAt, &personVal, &sectionsJSON)\n964\t\tif err != nil {\n965\t\t\t// If the query fails, it might be because sections_json column doesn't exist\n966\t\t\t// Try fallback query without sections_json\n967\t\t\tquery = `SELECT content, generated_at FROM briefings WHERE date = ?`\n968\t\t\targs = []interface{}{date}\n969\t\n970\t\t\tif person != \"\" {\n971\t\t\t\tquery += ` AND person = ?`\n972\t\t\t\targs = append(args, person)\n973\t\t\t} else {\n974\t\t\t\tquery += ` AND (person IS NULL OR person = '')`\n975\t\t\t}\n976\t\n977\t\t\tvar content2 string\n978\t\t\tvar generatedAt2 int64\n979\t\t\terr2 := g.db.QueryRow(query, args...).Scan(&content2, &generatedAt2)\n980\t\t\tif err2 != nil {\n981\t\t\t\treturn nil, err2\n982\t\t\t}\n983\t\t\tcontent = content2\n984\t\t\tgeneratedAt = generatedAt2\n985\t\t\t// personVal and sectionsJSON remain NULL/invalid\n986\t\t}\n987\t\n988\t\tb := &Briefing{\n989\t\t\tDate:        date,\n990\t\t\tPerson:      personVal.String,\n991\t\t\tContent:     content,\n992\t\t\tGeneratedAt: generatedAt,\n993\t\t}\n994\t\n995\t\t// Unmarshal sections if present\n996\t\tif sectionsJSON.Valid {\n997\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(sectionsJSON.String), &b.Sections); err != nil {\n998\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Failed to unmarshal sections for %s: %v\", date, err)\n999\t\t\t}\n1000\t\t}\n1001\t\n1002\t\treturn b, nil\n1003\t}\n1004\t\n1005\t// GetLatest retrieves the most recent briefing (for any person).\n1006\tfunc (g *Generator) GetLatest() (*Briefing, person,\n1036\t\t\tContent:     content,\n1037\t\t\tGeneratedAt: generatedAt,\n1038\t\t}\n1039\t\n1040\t\t// Unmarshal sections if present\n1041\t\tif sectionsJSON.Valid {\n1042\t\t\tif err := ShouldPushBriefing() bool {\n1143\t\tnow := time.Now()\n1144\t\thour := now.Hour()\n1145\t\n1146\t\t// Only push after 6am\n1147\t\tif hour < 6 {\n1148\t\t\treturn detection quality if not excellent\n\tif quality < 90 {\n\t\tcontentParts = append(contentParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"Detection quality: %.0f%%.\", quality))\n\t}\n\n\t// Skip if everything is healthy\n\tif len(contentParts) == 1 && online == total && quality >= 90 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tcontent := strings.Join(contentParts, \" \")\n\n\treturn &Section{\n\t\tType:     SectionTypeSystemHealth,\n\t\tContent:  content,\n\t\tPriority: 30,\n\t}\n}\n\n// generatePredictionBlock generates BLOCK 6 — Prediction hint.\nfunc (g *Generator) generatePredictionBlock(person generateOvernightEventsBlock(nightStart, nightEnd time.Time, person string) *Section {\n\t// Calculate quiet hours period\n\t// Use the passed time range directly (already calculated as 18:00 previous day to 06:00 current day)\n\n\tquery := `SELECT type, zone, person, detail_json, timestamp_ms, severity\n\t           FROM events\n\t           WHERE timestamp_ms >= ?
